<name>Thierry Trang<//name><date>1558758745147<//date><rate>5<//rate>< review>
Typical Chinese restaurant, similar to what may be found in Shanghai's old town gourmet districts. Mostly (but not exclusively!) spicy meals are served but the spicy level can be adjusted to taste. Generous quantities makes it very affordable. Plus, there are "order 4 get 1 free" types of offers which is perfect for family or friends dinners.< /review>

<review>This Place is great. I would highly recommend if you are interested in exploring diverse Chinese cuisine. It has both popular Americanized dishes like Kung Pao chicken and general Tso but also a large selection of more traditional dishes. All which are perfectly prepared. I have been here several times myself but most recently a took a Chinese friend and she loved it.

The peppercorn chicken is like an addiction. I can't wait for it to be served every time I order it. At first, I didn't know what the flavor description on the menu meant. Because, it said it has a numbing flavor. I thought it was a typo but you will be pleasantly surprised to find that it does have a nice mild numbing sensation after eating the Sichuan pepper oil that coats the zucchini and chicken. I truly think I'm addicted because I literally begin salivating when I see it knowing that I'll be getting that nice numbing effect.

This time, we also ordered the pork spam hot pot and it was delicious. And it's a huge bowl filled with a wide assortment of goodies and on the bottom was perfectly cooked glass noodles. It was altogether a real masterpiece.

These smaller places get so little attention but they blow away mainstream big name restaurants. I would like to keep it a secret but I really hope that it gets the recognition it deserves.< /review>< Time>
1545522728970</Time>

< review>
If you buy and pick up the day before Thanksgiving, give yourself about 40-60 minutes to wait in line.  Otherwise, pick it up 2 days before Thanksgiving because the ham will definitely be just as tasty (and smokey).  They also have turkey and a few other side items for sale, including Kings Hawaiian buns.  The parking lot isn't that big when it's crowded so you're better off parking across the street or in the nearby neighborhood and walking over.</review>

< text>
I can't believe I have passed Honey Baked Ham Company  5 days a week for a full year and never knew what it had to offer (Mind Blown)

As thanksgiving approaches I was talking to a co worker about my thoughts in purchasing a ham to only be told that they are open year round and also have lunch/dinner special.

On a lunch break I finally decided to stop by and see what they offer, it was about 12:30pm and as I waked in there was only one person in line so the wait time was very little which I was happy about only because I knew I had lots of questions. The staff was amazing and very helpful, they answered all my questions and suggested some of the popular items.

I ordered the Tavern Club with the Hawaiian Bread which cost $6.99 (What a Deal) and for $2.00 more you can make it a combo with a choice of a fresh made side and a side salad but right now they also have the $2.00 combo with a fresh made side and a slice of cake. This combo is a great buy and let me tell you it was sooo delicious. The ham is cooked to perfection and cut thick to make every bite worth your wild.

I am happy to announce that I work minutes away and will definitely be back during my lunch breaks to try everything on the menu.

FYI they have a good amount of parking out front and lots of staff to keep the flow moving inside.<//text>
